****************************The Chosen Cube*******************************
0,2,4,6,8,11,13,15,17,19,21,23,26,28,30,32,34,36,38,41,43,45,47,49,51,53,56,58,60,62,64,66,68,71,73,75,79,
***************************************************************************

The superpoly of this cube is the sum of all the remaining terms, where one 
remaining term equal to the product of all the polynomial in each blcok.  
Note that, one block ranges  from 
"<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<the i-th Remaining Term>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>"
to 
"<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<the (i+1)-th Remaining Term>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>"
